If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
MSC2290637757
On August 9, 2022, we sent a request for initial evidence for your Form I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number MSC2290637757. The request for evidence explains what we need from you. We will not take action on your case until we receive the evidence or the deadline to submit it expires. Please follow the instructions in the request for evidence. If you do not receive your request for evidence by August 24, 2022, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

The request for evidence explains what we need from you. We will not take action on your case until we receive the evidence or the deadline to submit it expires. Please follow the instructions in the request for evidence. If you do not receive your request for evidence by August 24, 2022, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy of the notice. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.

MSC2290604133
On August 9, 2022, we rejected your Form I-485, Application to Register Permanent Residence or Adjust Status, Receipt Number MSC2290604133 because your filing fee was returned by your financial institution for insufficient funds. Any previously assigned priority or processing date is no longer applicable. If you wish to still pursue the benefit, you must file a new application or petition and submit a new fee filing fee. If you need assistance, contact the USCIS Contact Center at www.uscis.gov/contactcenter. If you change your mailing address, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
